   (function (bugsnag) {

                'use strict';

                var readCookie = function (name) {
                    var nameEQ = name + "=";
                    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                    for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                        var c = ca[i];
                        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
                        if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
                    }
                    return null;
                };

  <script>
   (function(win, doc, style, timeout) {
           var STYLE_ID = 'at-body-style';

           function getParent() {
               return doc.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
           }

          function addStyle(parent, id, def) {
            if (!parent) {
              return;
            }

            var style = doc.createElement('style');
            style.id = id;
            style.innerHTML = def;
            parent.appendChild(style);
          }

          function removeStyle(parent, id) {
            if (!parent) {
              return;
            }

            var style = doc.getElementById(id);

            if (!style) {
              return;
            }

            parent.removeChild(style);
          }

          addStyle(getParent(), STYLE_ID, style);
          setTimeout(function() {
            removeStyle(getParent(), STYLE_ID);
          }, timeout);
       }(window, document, "body {opacity: 0 !important}", 3000));
  </script>

  <script>
   (function () {
        var publicPreRequireDependencies = {};
        window.prerequire = {
            storage: [],
            registerPublicDependency: function (name, value) {
                publicPreRequireDependencies[name] = value;
            },
            add: function add(dependencies, callback) {
                if (!(dependencies instanceof Array)) {
                    console.error('dependencies should be an Array');
                }
                this.storage.push({ dependencies: dependencies, callback: callback });
            },
            fire: function fire() {
                if (!window.flowFinished) {
                    return;
                }
                for (var i = 0, len = this.storage.length; i < len; i++) {
                    var requirements = this.storage[i];
                    tryCatch(function () {
                        requirements.callback.apply(
                            null,
                            requirements.dependencies.map(function (key, value) {
                                return publicPreRequireDependencies[key];
                            })
                        );
                    }, 'failed to run prerequired callback: ' + requirements.callback)();
                }
            }
        };

        window.tryCatch = function (fn, message) {
            message = message || '';
            if (window.DEBUG) {
                return function () {
                    var args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
                    fn.apply(this, args);
                };
            } else {
                return function () {
                    var errorDetails;
                    var args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
                    try {
                        fn.apply(this, args);
                    } catch (ex) {
                        if (typeof ex === 'string') {
                            errorDetails = ex;
                        } else {
                            errorDetails = {
                                errorType: ex.constructor,
                                message: ex.message,
                                stack: ex.stack
                            };
                        }
                        if (window.Bugsnag) {
                            Bugsnag.notify('Logic Error', message, {
                                ErrorDetails: errorDetails
                            });
                        } else {
                            throw ex;
                        }
                    }
                };
            }
        };
    }());
  </script>

            <script>
             (function(){
                        var appData = window.appData = window.appData || {};

                        function updateLink(className,links){

                            var elements = document.getElementsByClassName(className);

                            var href=links.info;

                            if (("; " + document.cookie).indexOf("; MembershipSession=") > -1){
                                href = links.manage
                            }

                            for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
                                elements[i].href = href;
                            }
                        }
                        appData.updateCustomerListUrls = function(){


                            var links ={
                                wishlist:{
                                    info: 'https://www.chapters.indigo.ca/en-ca/list/wishlist-howto',
                                    manage: 'https://www.chapters.indigo.ca/en-ca/list/manage/wishlist'
                                },
                                registry:{
                                    info: 'https://www.chapters.indigo.ca/en-ca/registry',
                                    manage: 'https://www.chapters.indigo.ca/en-ca/list/manage/registry'
                                }
                            }
                            updateLink("wishlist-nav",links.wishlist);
                            updateLink("registry-nav",links.registry);
                        }
                        appData.updateCustomerListUrls();
                	}())
            </script>

      </li>
      <li>
       If you do not have to customize your Internet security settings, click
       <strong>
        Default Level
       </strong>
       . Then go to step 5.
      </li>
      <li>
       If you have to customize your Internet security settings, follow steps a &amp; b, then go to step 5:
       <ol style="list-style:lower-alpha inside none; padding-left: 20px;">
        <li>
         Click
         <strong>
          Custom Level
         </strong>
         .
        </li>
        <li>
         In the
         <strong>
          Security Settings
         </strong>
         - Internet Zone dialog box, click Enable for Active Scripting in the Scripting section.
        </li>
       </ol>
      </li>
      <li>
       Click
       <strong>
        OK
       </strong>
       to close the
       <strong>
        Internet Options
       </strong>
       popup.
      </li>
      <li>
       <strong>
        Refresh your browser
       </strong>
       page to run scripts and reload content.
      </li>
     </ol>
     <p style="font: 30px/30px 'Gibson Regular', 'Helvetica', 'Arial', sans-serif; color:#333;">
      Chrome
     </p>
     <ol style="list-style:decimal inside none; margin: 10px 0 20px;">
      <li>
       On the
       <strong>
        Control
       </strong>
       button (top right of browser), select
       <strong>
        Settings
       </strong>
       from dropdown.
      </li>
      <li>
       Click on
       <strong>
        + Show advanced settings
       </strong>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       Under the header
       <strong>
        JavaScript
       </strong>
       select the following radio button:
       <strong>
        Allow all sites to run JavaScript (recommended)
       </strong>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       Click
       <strong>
        OK
       </strong>
       to close the
       <strong>
        Content Settings
       </strong>
       popup and close the
       <strong>
        Settings
       </strong>
       tab.
      </li>
      <li>
       <strong>
        Refresh your browser
       </strong>
       page to run scripts and reload content.
      </li>
     </ol>
    </div>
